Cooldown Manager​

note

This is quite simple and I am not using any sort of skins around the cooldown manager as of now. There are lots of options out there, but in my exprience it can make the UI very unstable. So until things smooth out I just use default (mostly).

Clean Cooldown Manager​

This centers the buff bar. Make sure your buffs are set to left aligned to keep the order intact. Feel free to tweak more settings in (/ccm).
